        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForThisReference implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader {
            private final net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType;

            public ForThisReference(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType) {
                this.instrumentedType = instrumentedType;
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription target, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {

                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot assign " + instrumentedType) + " to ") + target);
                }
                return stackManipulation;
            }

            public enum Factory implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory {

                INSTANCE;
                @java.lang.Override
                public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                    return instrumentedType;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> make(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod) {
                    if (instrumentedMethod.isStatic()) {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException(instrumentedMethod + " is static and cannot supply an invoker instance");
                    }
                    return java.util.Collections.<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>singletonList(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForThisReference(instrumentedType));
                }
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForInstrumentedType implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader {
            private final net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType;

            public ForInstrumentedType(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType) {
                this.instrumentedType = instrumentedType;
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription target, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.ClassConstant.of(instrumentedType), assigner.assign(new net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription.Generic.OfNonGenericType.ForLoadedType(java.lang.Class.class), target.getType(), typing));
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException("Cannot assign Class value to " + target);
                }
                return stackManipulation;
            }

            public enum Factory implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory {

                    return java.util.Collections.<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>singletonList(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForInstrumentedType(instrumentedType));
                }
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForMethodParameter implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader {
            private final int index;

            private final net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod;

            public ForMethodParameter(int index, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod) {
                this.index = index;
                this.instrumentedMethod = instrumentedMethod;
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription target, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription parameterDescription = instrumentedMethod.getParameters().get(index);
                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodVariableAccess.load(parameterDescription), assigner.assign(parameterDescription.getType(), target.getType(), typing));
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((((("Cannot assign " + parameterDescription) + " to ") + target) + " for ") + instrumentedMethod);
                }
                return stackManipulation;
            }

            protected enum OfInstrumentedMethod implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory {

                INSTANCE;
                @java.lang.Override
                public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                    return instrumentedType;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> make(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod) {
                    java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> argumentLoaders = new java.util.ArrayList<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>(instrumentedMethod.getParameters().size());
                    for (net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription parameterDescription : instrumentedMethod.getParameters()) {
                        argumentLoaders.add(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForMethodParameter(parameterDescription.getIndex(), instrumentedMethod));
                    }
                    return argumentLoaders;
                }
            }

            @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
            protected static class Factory implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory {
                private final int index;

                public Factory(int index) {
                    this.index = index;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                    return instrumentedType;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> make(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod) {
                    if (index >= instrumentedMethod.getParameters().size()) {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((instrumentedMethod + " does not have a parameter with index ") + index);
                    }
                    return java.util.Collections.<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>singletonList(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForMethodParameter(index, instrumentedMethod));
                }
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForMethodParameterArray implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader {
            private final net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterList<?> parameters;

            public ForMethodParameterArray(net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterList<?> parameters) {
                this.parameters = parameters;
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription target, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription.Generic componentType;
                if (target.getType().represents(java.lang.Object.class)) {
                    componentType = net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription.Generic.OBJECT;
                } else
                    if (target.getType().isArray()) {
                        componentType = target.getType().getComponentType();
                    } else {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException();
                    }

                java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation> stackManipulations = new java.util.ArrayList<net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation>(parameters.size());
                for (net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription parameter : parameters) {
                    net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodVariableAccess.load(parameter), assigner.assign(parameter.getType(), componentType, typing));
                    if (stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                        stackManipulations.add(stackManipulation);
                    } else {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot assign " + parameter) + " to ") + componentType);
                    }
                }
                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.collection.ArrayFactory.forType(componentType).withValues(stackManipulations));
            }

            public enum ForInstrumentedMethod implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory {

                INSTANCE;
                @java.lang.Override
                public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                    return instrumentedType;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> make(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod) {
                    return java.util.Collections.<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>singletonList(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForMethodParameterArray(instrumentedMethod.getParameters()));
                }
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForMethodParameterArrayElement implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader {
            private final net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription parameterDescription;

            private final int index;

            public ForMethodParameterArrayElement(net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription parameterDescription, int index) {
                this.parameterDescription = parameterDescription;
                this.index = index;
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription target, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodVariableAccess.load(parameterDescription), net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.IntegerConstant.forValue(index), net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.collection.ArrayAccess.of(parameterDescription.getType().getComponentType()).load(), assigner.assign(parameterDescription.getType().getComponentType(), target.getType(), typing));
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot assign " + parameterDescription.getType().getComponentType()) + " to ") + target);
                }
                return stackManipulation;
            }

            @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
            protected static class OfParameter implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory {
                private final int index;

                private final int arrayIndex;

                public OfParameter(int index, int arrayIndex) {
                    this.index = index;
                    this.arrayIndex = arrayIndex;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                    return instrumentedType;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> make(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod) {
                    if (instrumentedMethod.getParameters().size() <= index) {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((instrumentedMethod + " does not declare a parameter with index ") + index);
                    } else
                        if (!instrumentedMethod.getParameters().get(index).getType().isArray()) {
                            throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException("Cannot access an item from non-array parameter " + instrumentedMethod.getParameters().get(index));
                        }

                    return java.util.Collections.<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>singletonList(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForMethodParameterArrayElement(instrumentedMethod.getParameters().get(index), arrayIndex));
                }
            }

            @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
            public static class OfInvokedMethod implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory {
                private final int index;

                public OfInvokedMethod(int index) {
                    this.index = index;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                    return instrumentedType;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> make(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod) {
                    if (instrumentedMethod.getParameters().size() <= index) {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((instrumentedMethod + " does not declare a parameter with index ") + index);
                    } else
                        if (!instrumentedMethod.getParameters().get(index).getType().isArray()) {
                            throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException("Cannot access an item from non-array parameter " + instrumentedMethod.getParameters().get(index));
                        }

                    java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> argumentLoaders = new java.util.ArrayList<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>(instrumentedMethod.getParameters().size());
                    for (int index = 0; index < invokedMethod.getParameters().size(); index++) {
                        argumentLoaders.add(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForMethodParameterArrayElement(instrumentedMethod.getParameters().get(this.index), index++));
                    }
                    return argumentLoaders;
                }
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForInstance implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader {
            private final net.bytebuddy.description.field.FieldDescription fieldDescription;

            public ForInstance(net.bytebuddy.description.field.FieldDescription fieldDescription) {
                this.fieldDescription = fieldDescription;
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription target, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.FieldAccess.forField(fieldDescription).read(), assigner.assign(fieldDescription.getType(), target.getType(), typing));
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot assign " + fieldDescription.getType()) + " to ") + target);
                }
                return stackManipulation;
            }

            @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode(exclude = "name")
            protected static class Factory implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory {
                private static final java.lang.String FIELD_PREFIX = "methodCall";

                private final java.lang.Object value;

                private final java.lang.String name;

                public Factory(java.lang.Object value) {
                    this.value = value;
                    name = (net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForInstance.Factory.FIELD_PREFIX + "$") + net.bytebuddy.utility.RandomString.make();
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                    return instrumentedType.withField(new net.bytebuddy.description.field.FieldDescription.Token(name, (org.objectweb.asm.Opcodes.ACC_SYNTHETIC | org.objectweb.asm.Opcodes.ACC_PUBLIC) | org.objectweb.asm.Opcodes.ACC_STATIC, new net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription.Generic.OfNonGenericType.ForLoadedType(value.getClass()))).withInitializer(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.LoadedTypeInitializer.ForStaticField(name, value));
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> make(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod) {
                    return java.util.Collections.<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>singletonList(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForInstance(instrumentedType.getDeclaredFields().filter(net.bytebuddy.matcher.ElementMatchers.named(name)).getOnly()));
                }
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForField implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader {
            private final net.bytebuddy.description.field.FieldDescription fieldDescription;

            private final net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod;

            public ForField(net.bytebuddy.description.field.FieldDescription fieldDescription, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod) {
                this.fieldDescription = fieldDescription;
                this.instrumentedMethod = instrumentedMethod;
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription target, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                if ((!fieldDescription.isStatic()) && instrumentedMethod.isStatic()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot access non-static " + fieldDescription) + " from ") + instrumentedMethod);
                }
                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(fieldDescription.isStatic() ? net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Trivial.INSTANCE : net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodVariableAccess.loadThis(), net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.FieldAccess.forField(fieldDescription).read(), assigner.assign(fieldDescription.getType(), target.getType(), typing));
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot assign " + fieldDescription) + " to ") + target);
                }
                return stackManipulation;
            }

            @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
            protected static class Factory implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory {
                private final java.lang.String name;

                private final net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.FieldLocator.Factory fieldLocatorFactory;

                public Factory(java.lang.String name, net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.FieldLocator.Factory fieldLocatorFactory) {
                    this.name = name;
                    this.fieldLocatorFactory = fieldLocatorFactory;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                    return instrumentedType;
                }

                @java.lang.Override
                public java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> make(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod) {
                    net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.FieldLocator.Resolution resolution = fieldLocatorFactory.make(instrumentedType).locate(name);
                    if (!resolution.isResolved()) {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Could not locate field '" + name) + "' on ") + instrumentedType);
                    }
                    return java.util.Collections.<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>singletonList(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForField(resolution.getField(), instrumentedMethod));
                }
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForStackManipulation implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader , net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory {
            private final net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation;

            private final net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDefinition typeDefinition;

            public ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation, java.lang.reflect.Type type) {
                this(stackManipulation, net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDefinition.Sort.describe(type));
            }

            public ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation, net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDefinition typeDefinition) {
                this.stackManipulation = stackManipulation;
                this.typeDefinition = typeDefinition;
            }

            public static net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory of(java.lang.Object value) {
                if (value == null) {
                    return net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForNullConstant.INSTANCE;
                } else
                    if (value instanceof java.lang.String) {
                        return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.TextConstant(((java.lang.String) (value))), java.lang.String.class);
                    } else
                        if (value instanceof java.lang.Boolean) {
                            return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.IntegerConstant.forValue(((java.lang.Boolean) (value))), boolean.class);
                        } else
                            if (value instanceof java.lang.Byte) {
                                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.IntegerConstant.forValue(((java.lang.Byte) (value))), byte.class);
                            } else
                                if (value instanceof java.lang.Short) {
                                    return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.IntegerConstant.forValue(((java.lang.Short) (value))), short.class);
                                } else
                                    if (value instanceof java.lang.Character) {
                                        return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.IntegerConstant.forValue(((java.lang.Character) (value))), char.class);
                                    } else
                                        if (value instanceof java.lang.Integer) {
                                            return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.IntegerConstant.forValue(((java.lang.Integer) (value))), int.class);
                                        } else
                                            if (value instanceof java.lang.Long) {
                                                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.LongConstant.forValue(((java.lang.Long) (value))), long.class);
                                            } else
                                                if (value instanceof java.lang.Float) {
                                                    return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.FloatConstant.forValue(((java.lang.Float) (value))), float.class);
                                                } else
                                                    if (value instanceof java.lang.Double) {
                                                        return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.DoubleConstant.forValue(((java.lang.Double) (value))), double.class);
                                                    } else
                                                        if (value instanceof java.lang.Class) {
                                                            return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.constant.ClassConstant.of(new net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription.ForLoadedType(((java.lang.Class<?>) (value)))), java.lang.Class.class);
                                                        } else
                                                            if (net.bytebuddy.utility.JavaType.METHOD_HANDLE.getTypeStub().isInstance(value)) {
                                                                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.utility.JavaConstant.MethodHandle.ofLoaded(value).asStackManipulation(), net.bytebuddy.utility.JavaType.METHOD_HANDLE.getTypeStub());
                                                            } else
                                                                if (net.bytebuddy.utility.JavaType.METHOD_TYPE.getTypeStub().isInstance(value)) {
                                                                    return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.utility.JavaConstant.MethodType.ofLoaded(value).asStackManipulation(), net.bytebuddy.utility.JavaType.METHOD_TYPE.getTypeStub());
                                                                } else
                                                                    if (value instanceof java.lang.Enum<?>) {
                                                                        net.bytebuddy.description.enumeration.EnumerationDescription enumerationDescription = new net.bytebuddy.description.enumeration.EnumerationDescription.ForLoadedEnumeration(((java.lang.Enum<?>) (value)));
                                                                        return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForStackManipulation(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.FieldAccess.forEnumeration(enumerationDescription), enumerationDescription.getEnumerationType());
                                                                    } else {
                                                                        return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.ForInstance.Factory(value);
                                                                    }













            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                return instrumentedType;
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> make(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod) {
                return java.util.Collections.<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>singletonList(this);
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription target, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation assigment = assigner.assign(typeDefinition.asGenericType(), target.getType(), typing);
                if (!assigment.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot assign " + target) + " to ") + typeDefinition);
                }
                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(stackManipulation, assigment);
            }
        }
    }

    protected interface TargetHandler extends net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType.Prepareable {
        net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing);

        enum ForSelfOrStaticInvocation implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler {

            INSTANCE;
            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(invokedMethod.isStatic() ? net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Trivial.INSTANCE : net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodVariableAccess.loadThis(), invokedMethod.isConstructor() ? net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.Duplication.SINGLE : net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Trivial.INSTANCE);
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                return instrumentedType;
            }
        }

        enum ForConstructingInvocation implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler {

            INSTANCE;
            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.TypeCreation.of(invokedMethod.getDeclaringType().asErasure()), net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.Duplication.SINGLE);
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                return instrumentedType;
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode(exclude = "name")
        class ForValue implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler {
            private static final java.lang.String FIELD_PREFIX = "invocationTarget";

            private final java.lang.Object target;

            private final net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription.Generic fieldType;

            private final java.lang.String name;

            protected ForValue(java.lang.Object target, net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription.Generic fieldType) {
                this.target = target;
                this.fieldType = fieldType;
                name = (net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler.ForValue.FIELD_PREFIX + "$") + net.bytebuddy.utility.RandomString.make();
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = assigner.assign(fieldType, invokedMethod.getDeclaringType().asGenericType(), typing);
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " on ") + fieldType);
                }
                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.FieldAccess.forField(instrumentedType.getDeclaredFields().filter(net.bytebuddy.matcher.ElementMatchers.named(name)).getOnly()).read(), stackManipulation);
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                return instrumentedType.withField(new net.bytebuddy.description.field.FieldDescription.Token(name, ((org.objectweb.asm.Opcodes.ACC_PUBLIC | org.objectweb.asm.Opcodes.ACC_STATIC) | org.objectweb.asm.Opcodes.ACC_VOLATILE) | org.objectweb.asm.Opcodes.ACC_SYNTHETIC, fieldType)).withInitializer(new net.bytebuddy.implementation.LoadedTypeInitializer.ForStaticField(name, target));
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForField implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler {
            private final java.lang.String name;

            private final net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.FieldLocator.Factory fieldLocatorFactory;

            protected ForField(java.lang.String name, net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.FieldLocator.Factory fieldLocatorFactory) {
                this.name = name;
                this.fieldLocatorFactory = fieldLocatorFactory;
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.FieldLocator.Resolution resolution = fieldLocatorFactory.make(instrumentedType).locate(name);
                if (!resolution.isResolved()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Could not locate field name " + name) + " on ") + instrumentedType);
                } else
                    if ((!resolution.getField().isStatic()) && (!instrumentedType.isAssignableTo(resolution.getField().getDeclaringType().asErasure()))) {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot access " + resolution.getField()) + " from ") + instrumentedType);
                    } else
                        if (!invokedMethod.isInvokableOn(resolution.getField().getType().asErasure())) {
                            throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " on ") + resolution.getField());
                        } else
                            if (!invokedMethod.isAccessibleTo(instrumentedType)) {
                                throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot access " + invokedMethod) + " from ") + instrumentedType);
                            }



                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = assigner.assign(resolution.getField().getType(), invokedMethod.getDeclaringType().asGenericType(), typing);
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " on ") + resolution.getField());
                }
                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(invokedMethod.isStatic() ? net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Trivial.INSTANCE : net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodVariableAccess.loadThis(), net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.FieldAccess.forField(resolution.getField()).read(), stackManipulation);
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                return instrumentedType;
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForMethodParameter implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler {
            private final int index;

            protected ForMethodParameter(int index) {
                this.index = index;
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription instrumentedType, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                if (instrumentedMethod.getParameters().size() < index) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalArgumentException((instrumentedMethod + " does not have a parameter with index ") + index);
                }
                net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription parameterDescription = instrumentedMethod.getParameters().get(index);
                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = assigner.assign(parameterDescription.getType(), invokedMethod.getDeclaringType().asGenericType(), typing);
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " on ") + parameterDescription.getType());
                }
                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodVariableAccess.load(parameterDescription), stackManipulation);
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType prepare(net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.InstrumentedType instrumentedType) {
                return instrumentedType;
            }
        }
    }

    protected interface MethodInvoker {
        net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation invoke(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.implementation.Implementation.Target implementationTarget);

        enum ForContextualInvocation implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker {

            INSTANCE;
            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation invoke(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.implementation.Implementation.Target implementationTarget) {
                if (invokedMethod.isVirtual() && (!invokedMethod.isInvokableOn(implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType()))) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " on ") + implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType());
                }
                return invokedMethod.isVirtual() ? net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodInvocation.invoke(invokedMethod).virtual(implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType()) : net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodInvocation.invoke(invokedMethod);
            }
        }

        @lombok.EqualsAndHashCode
        class ForVirtualInvocation implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker {
            private final net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription typeDescription;

            protected ForVirtualInvocation(net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription typeDescription) {
                this.typeDescription = typeDescription;
            }

            protected ForVirtualInvocation(java.lang.Class<?> type) {
                this(new net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription.ForLoadedType(type));
            }

            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation invoke(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.implementation.Implementation.Target implementationTarget) {
                if (!invokedMethod.isVirtual()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException(("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " virtually");
                } else
                    if (!invokedMethod.isInvokableOn(typeDescription.asErasure())) {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " on ") + typeDescription);
                    } else
                        if (!typeDescription.asErasure().isAccessibleTo(implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType())) {
                            throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((typeDescription + " is not accessible to ") + implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType());
                        }


                return net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodInvocation.invoke(invokedMethod).virtual(typeDescription.asErasure());
            }

            public enum WithImplicitType implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker {

                INSTANCE;
                @java.lang.Override
                public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation invoke(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.implementation.Implementation.Target implementationTarget) {
                    if (!invokedMethod.isVirtual()) {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException(("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " virtually");
                    }
                    return net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodInvocation.invoke(invokedMethod);
                }
            }
        }

        enum ForSuperMethodInvocation implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker {

            INSTANCE;
            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation invoke(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.implementation.Implementation.Target implementationTarget) {
                if (implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType().getSuperClass() == null) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException("Cannot invoke super method for " + implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType());
                } else
                    if (!invokedMethod.isInvokableOn(implementationTarget.getOriginType().asErasure())) {
                        throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " as super method of ") + implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType());
                    }

                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = implementationTarget.invokeDominant(invokedMethod.asSignatureToken());
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException(("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " as a super method");
                }
                return stackManipulation;
            }
        }

        enum ForDefaultMethodInvocation implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker {

            INSTANCE;
            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation invoke(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.implementation.Implementation.Target implementationTarget) {
                if (!invokedMethod.isInvokableOn(implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType())) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " as default method of ") + implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType());
                }
                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = implementationTarget.invokeDefault(invokedMethod.asSignatureToken(), invokedMethod.getDeclaringType().asErasure());
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " on ") + implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType());
                }
                return stackManipulation;
            }
        }
    }

    protected enum TerminationHandler {

        RETURNING() {
            @java.lang.Override
            public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation stackManipulation = assigner.assign(invokedMethod.isConstructor() ? invokedMethod.getDeclaringType().asGenericType() : invokedMethod.getReturnType(), instrumentedMethod.getReturnType(), typing);
                if (!stackManipulation.isValid()) {
                    throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot return " + invokedMethod.getReturnType()) + " from ") + instrumentedMethod);
                }
                return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(stackManipulation, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.member.MethodReturn.of(instrumentedMethod.getReturnType()));
            }
        },
        DROPPING() {
            @java.lang.Override
            protected net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing) {
                return net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.Removal.of(invokedMethod.isConstructor() ? invokedMethod.getDeclaringType() : invokedMethod.getReturnType());
            }
        };
        protected abstract net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation resolve(net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner assigner, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing typing);
    }

    public static class WithoutSpecifiedTarget extends net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall {
        protected WithoutSpecifiedTarget(net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodLocator methodLocator) {
            super(methodLocator, net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler.ForSelfOrStaticInvocation.INSTANCE, java.util.Collections.<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory>emptyList(), net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker.ForContextualInvocation.INSTANCE, net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TerminationHandler.RETURNING, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.DEFAULT, net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.assign.Assigner.Typing.STATIC);
        }

        @java.lang.SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
        public net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall on(java.lang.Object target) {
            return on(target, ((java.lang.Class) (target.getClass())));
        }

        public <T> net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall on(T target, java.lang.Class<? super T> type) {
            return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall(methodLocator, new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler.ForValue(target, new net.bytebuddy.description.type.TypeDescription.Generic.OfNonGenericType.ForLoadedType(type)), argumentLoaders, new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker.ForVirtualInvocation(type), terminationHandler, assigner, typing);
        }

        public net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall onArgument(int index) {
            if (index < 0) {
                throw new java.lang.IllegalArgumentException("An argument index cannot be negative: " + index);
            }
            return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall(methodLocator, new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler.ForMethodParameter(index), argumentLoaders, net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker.ForVirtualInvocation.WithImplicitType.INSTANCE, terminationHandler, assigner, typing);
        }

        public net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall onField(java.lang.String name) {
            return onField(name, net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.FieldLocator.ForClassHierarchy.Factory.INSTANCE);
        }

        public net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall onField(java.lang.String name, net.bytebuddy.dynamic.scaffold.FieldLocator.Factory fieldLocatorFactory) {
            return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall(methodLocator, new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler.ForField(name, fieldLocatorFactory), argumentLoaders, net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker.ForVirtualInvocation.WithImplicitType.INSTANCE, terminationHandler, assigner, typing);
        }

        public net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall onSuper() {
            return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall(methodLocator, net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler.ForSelfOrStaticInvocation.INSTANCE, argumentLoaders, net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker.ForSuperMethodInvocation.INSTANCE, terminationHandler, assigner, typing);
        }

        public net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall onDefault() {
            return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall(methodLocator, net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.TargetHandler.ForSelfOrStaticInvocation.INSTANCE, argumentLoaders, net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.MethodInvoker.ForDefaultMethodInvocation.INSTANCE, terminationHandler, assigner, typing);
        }
    }

    protected class Appender implements net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.ByteCodeAppender {
        private final net.bytebuddy.implementation.Implementation.Target implementationTarget;

        protected Appender(net.bytebuddy.implementation.Implementation.Target implementationTarget) {
            this.implementationTarget = implementationTarget;
        }

        @java.lang.Override
        public net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.ByteCodeAppender.Size apply(org.objectweb.asm.MethodVisitor methodVisitor, net.bytebuddy.implementation.Implementation.Context implementationContext, net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription instrumentedMethod) {
            net.bytebuddy.description.method.MethodDescription invokedMethod = methodLocator.resolve(implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType(), instrumentedMethod);
            if (!invokedMethod.isVisibleTo(implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType())) {
                throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException((("Cannot invoke " + invokedMethod) + " from ") + implementationContext.getInstrumentedType());
            }
            java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader> argumentLoaders = new java.util.ArrayList<net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader>(net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.this.argumentLoaders.size());
            for (net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader.Factory argumentLoader : net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.this.argumentLoaders) {
                argumentLoaders.addAll(argumentLoader.make(implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType(), instrumentedMethod, invokedMethod));
            }
            net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterList<?> parameters = invokedMethod.getParameters();
            java.util.Iterator<? extends net.bytebuddy.description.method.ParameterDescription> parameterIterator = parameters.iterator();
            if (parameters.size() != argumentLoaders.size()) {
                throw new java.lang.IllegalStateException(((invokedMethod + " does not take ") + argumentLoaders.size()) + " arguments");
            }
            java.util.List<net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation> argumentInstructions = new java.util.ArrayList<net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation>(argumentLoaders.size());
            for (net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.ArgumentLoader argumentLoader : argumentLoaders) {
                argumentInstructions.add(argumentLoader.resolve(parameterIterator.next(), assigner, typing));
            }
            net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Size size = new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(targetHandler.resolve(invokedMethod, instrumentedMethod, implementationTarget.getInstrumentedType(), assigner, typing), new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.StackManipulation.Compound(argumentInstructions), methodInvoker.invoke(invokedMethod, implementationTarget), terminationHandler.resolve(invokedMethod, instrumentedMethod, assigner, typing)).apply(methodVisitor, implementationContext);
            return new net.bytebuddy.implementation.bytecode.ByteCodeAppender.Size(size.getMaximalSize(), instrumentedMethod.getStackSize());
        }

        private net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall getOuter() {
            return net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.this;
        }

        @java.lang.Override
        public boolean equals(java.lang.Object other) {
            if (this == other)
                return true;

            if ((other == null) || (getClass() != other.getClass()))
                return false;

            net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.Appender appender = ((net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.Appender) (other));
            return implementationTarget.equals(appender.implementationTarget) && net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.this.equals(appender.getOuter());
        }

        @java.lang.Override
        public int hashCode() {
            return implementationTarget.hashCode() + (31 * net.bytebuddy.implementation.MethodCall.this.hashCode());
        }
    }
